<div id="review_1337746624" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1337746624" />
    <a title="Jody " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/41767362-jody"><img alt="Jody " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1558120407p2/41767362.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1337746624?book_show_action=true">Oct 07, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jody " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jody " href="/user/show/41767362-jody">Jody </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/41767362-jody?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1337746624" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8445650872441224624">I have been anticipating getting to this series for some time now, and I’m glad I finally did. This is an epic story of good versus evil at its finest. The world building had a unique quality that set it apart from other series in this genre. The characters were well developed and interesting. It did take me a little longer than usual to get familiar with all of the characters and kingdoms, but with the magnitude of characters and information in this story it is to be expected. At least for me a</span>
  <span id="freeText8445650872441224624" style="display:none">I have been anticipating getting to this series for some time now, and I’m glad I finally did. This is an epic story of good versus evil at its finest. The world building had a unique quality that set it apart from other series in this genre. The characters were well developed and interesting. It did take me a little longer than usual to get familiar with all of the characters and kingdoms, but with the magnitude of characters and information in this story it is to be expected. At least for me anyway!<br /><br />I really enjoyed the many different POV’s. There is a lot going on in the book, and Mr. Gwynne does a great job of spending time with each character to give you as much information as possible. The sub characters that didn’t have a POV in the book were just as interesting. I’m hoping we get some of their POV’s in the next books. Especially Brina and Gar!<br /><br />The story itself is as bloody and ruthless as it gets. Don’t get too attached to any of the characters, because you don’t know when their time is up. Mr. Gwynne is like the grim reaper dealing death where he sees fit. I am wondering if anyone is going to be left when this is all over. <br /> <br />This was one of my favorite reads of the year, possibly ever. I enjoyed it that much. Thank you Mr. Gwynne for such a fantastic read! I can’t wait to see where the story goes from here.<br /><br />5 stars!!!! <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="8445650872441224624" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

The amount of names thrown at you throughout the first half of the book was a bit overwhelming, but I got used to it and now I'm pretty much familiar with all of them. The thing about this book is that it's written in multiple POV's which made it easy for me to connect with the characters, good and bad although such a thing doesn't really exist here.   <span id="freeText18321959614572067362" style="display:none"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1394990763ra/8932795.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Holy. Fucking. Shit.</b> Those last 100 pages or so just sealed the five star deal for me. The amount of names thrown at you throughout the first half of the book was a bit overwhelming, but I got used to it and now I'm pretty much familiar with all of them. The thing about this book is that it's written in multiple POV's which made it easy for me to connect with the characters, good and bad although such a thing doesn't really exist here. They all have their own ambitions and reasons as to why they seek to destroy one another. And that's what made this such an enjoyable and thrilling read to me. What started as a slow-paced read turned out to be a character-driven, explosive, murderous book with a huge amount of potential for the other books in this series. I'm seriously so hooked! <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1499186634ra/23202579.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>

	<tr>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('V9ZA02UZYEiXDMBSCS1zNilcaEeB39KThOMhsz0cYt+9CWU6Mfvd7Xd6rM7W83uMWwkw6TAk285xzAMb+iHXoA==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('jwYBc8cj7qOdBo7nkbBfE7qi91aXVaIEV0M4VgB22Axl2SSak8FTBn1w4ntOblepyPev+Cauq1mibBr+x0ttcw==')})
  }

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer6617196818113379027">Malice is my debut novel. Goldsboro Books of London, specialists in signed first-editions, have made Malice their 'Book of the Month' for December 2012.<br/><br/>I was born in Singapore while my dad was stationed there in the RAF. Up until he retired that meant a lot of traveling around, generally a move every three years or so.<br/><br/>I live with my wife and four wonderful (and demanding) children in East Sussex. </span>
  <span id="freeText6617196818113379027" style="display:none">Malice is my debut novel. Goldsboro Books of London, specialists in signed first-editions, have made Malice their 'Book of the Month' for December 2012.<br /><br />I was born in Singapore while my dad was stationed there in the RAF. Up until he retired that meant a lot of traveling around, generally a move every three years or so.<br /><br />I live with my wife and four wonderful (and demanding) children in East Sussex. Also three dogs, two of which will chew anything that stands still. I have had many strange and wonderful jobs, including packing soap in a soap factory, waitering in a french restaurant in Canada, playing double bass in a rock n roll band, and lecturing at Brighton University.<br /><br />I stepped out of university work due to my daughter’s disability, so now I split my time caring for her and working from home - I work with my wife rejuvenating vintage furniture, which means fixing, lifting, carrying, painting and generally doing what my wife tells me to do...<br /><br />And somehow during this time I started writing. I’ve always told my children stories at bed-time, and they pestered long and hard for me to write some of it down. At the same time I felt that my brain was switching off a little - vintage furniture is my wife’s passion, whereas my passions are geekier!<br /><br />That’s how The Banished Lands and Malice began, though along the way it became more than just a hobby. I’m still in shock that it is actually a real book, rather than just pages on my desk. <br /><br /></span>
